(*********************************************************************************

 Displayed monoidal categories

 In this file, we define the notion of a displayed monoidal category. The style of
 the definition is similar to the definition of a monoidal category.

Note: after refactoring on March 10, 2023, the prior Git history of this development is found via
git log -- UniMath/CategoryTheory/Monoidal/DisplayedMonoidalWhiskered.v

 *********************************************************************************)

Section DisplayedMonoidalCategories.

  Definition disp_tensor
             {C : category}
             (D : disp_cat C)
             (M : monoidal C)
    : UU
    := disp_bifunctor M D D D.

  Identity Coercion disptensor_into_dispbifunctor : disp_tensor >-> disp_bifunctor.

  Definition disp_leftunitor_data
             {C : category}
             {D : disp_cat C}
             {M : monoidal C}
             (DT : disp_tensor D M)
             (i : D I_{M})
    : UU
    := ∏ (x : C) (xx : D x), i ⊗⊗_{DT} xx -->[lu^{M}_{x}] xx.

  Definition disp_leftunitorinv_data
             {C : category}
             {D : disp_cat C}
             {M : monoidal C}
             (DT : disp_tensor D M)
             (i : D I_{M})
    : UU
    := ∏ (x : C) (xx : D x), xx -->[luinv^{M}_{x}] i ⊗⊗_{DT} xx.

  Definition disp_rightunitor_data
             {C : category}
             {D : disp_cat C}
             {M : monoidal C}
             (DT : disp_tensor D M)
             (i : D I_{M})
    : UU
    := ∏ (x : C) (xx : D x), xx ⊗⊗_{DT} i -->[ru^{M}_{x}] xx.

  Definition disp_rightunitorinv_data
             {C : category}
             {D : disp_cat C}
             {M : monoidal C}
             (DT : disp_tensor D M)
             (i : D I_{M})
    : UU
    := ∏ (x : C) (xx : D x), xx -->[ruinv^{M}_{x}] xx ⊗⊗_{DT} i.

  Definition disp_associator_data
             {C : category}
             {D : disp_cat C}
             {M : monoidal C}
             (DT : disp_tensor D M)
    : UU
    := ∏ (x y z : C) (xx : D x) (yy : D y) (zz : D z),
       (xx ⊗⊗_{DT} yy) ⊗⊗_{DT} zz
       -->[α^{M}_{x,y,z}]
       xx ⊗⊗_{DT} (yy ⊗⊗_{DT} zz).

  Definition disp_associatorinv_data
             {C : category}
             {D : disp_cat C}
             {M : monoidal C}
             (DT : disp_tensor D M)
    : UU
    := ∏ (x y z : C) (xx : D x) (yy : D y) (zz : D z),
       xx ⊗⊗_{DT} (yy ⊗⊗_{DT} zz)
       -->[αinv_{M} x y z]
       (xx ⊗⊗_{DT} yy) ⊗⊗_{DT} zz.

  Definition disp_monoidal_data
             {C : category}
             (D : disp_cat C)
             (M : monoidal C)
    : UU
    := ∑ (DT : disp_tensor D M)
         (i : D I_{M}),
       (disp_leftunitor_data DT i)
       × (disp_leftunitorinv_data DT i)
       × (disp_rightunitor_data DT i)
       × (disp_rightunitorinv_data DT i)
       × (disp_associator_data DT)
       × (disp_associatorinv_data DT).

M: monoidal C

i: D I_{ M}
dlu: disp_leftunitor_data DT i
dru: disp_rightunitor_data DT i
dα: disp_associator_data DT
disp_monoidal_data D M

xx: D x
aux:= gdisp (leftwhiskering_functor M I_{ M} x)
  (functor_identity C x)
  (pr1 (leftunitor_nat_z_iso M) x)
  (pr2 (leftunitor_nat_z_iso M) x)
  (i ⊗⊗_{ DT} xx) xx (dlu x xx): is_z_iso_disp
  (make_z_iso' (pr1 (leftunitor_nat_z_iso M) x)
     (pr2 (leftunitor_nat_z_iso M) x))
  (dlu x xx)
xx -->[ luinv^{ M }_{ x}] i ⊗⊗_{ DT} xx

      exact (pr1 aux).

C: category
D: disp_cat C
gdisp: groupoidal_disp_cat D
M: monoidal C
DT: disp_tensor D M
i: D I_{ M}
dlu: disp_leftunitor_data DT i
dru: disp_rightunitor_data DT i
dα: disp_associator_data DT
(λ _ : disp_rightunitorinv_data DT i,
 disp_associator_data DT × disp_associatorinv_data DT)
  ((λ (x : C) (xx : D x),
    let aux :=
      gdisp (rightwhiskering_functor M I_{ M} x)
        (functor_identity C x)
        (pr1 (rightunitor_nat_z_iso M) x)
        (pr2 (rightunitor_nat_z_iso M) x)
        (xx ⊗⊗_{ DT} i) xx (dru x xx) in
    pr1 aux)
   :
   disp_rightunitorinv_data DT i)

    
C: category
D: disp_cat C
gdisp: groupoidal_disp_cat D
M: monoidal C
DT: disp_tensor D M

C: category
D: disp_cat C
gdisp: groupoidal_disp_cat D
M: monoidal C
DT: disp_tensor D M
i: D I_{ M}
dlu: disp_leftunitor_data DT i
dru: disp_rightunitor_data DT i
dα: disp_associator_data DT
x, y, z: C
xx: D x
yy: D y
zz: D z
xx ⊗⊗_{ DT} (yy ⊗⊗_{ DT} zz) -->[
αinv^{ M }_{ x, y, z}] (xx ⊗⊗_{ DT} yy) ⊗⊗_{ DT} zz

    
C: category
D: disp_cat C
gdisp: groupoidal_disp_cat D
M: monoidal C
DT: disp_tensor D M
i: D I_{ M}
dlu: disp_leftunitor_data DT i
dru: disp_rightunitor_data DT i
dα: disp_associator_data DT
x, y, z: C
xx: D x
yy: D y
zz: D z
aux:= gdisp
  (bifunctor_on_objects M
     (bifunctor_on_objects M x y) z)
  (bifunctor_on_objects M x
     (bifunctor_on_objects M y z))
  (pr1 (z_iso_from_associator_iso M x y z))
  (pr2 (z_iso_from_associator_iso M x y z))
  ((xx ⊗⊗_{ DT} yy) ⊗⊗_{ DT} zz)
  (xx ⊗⊗_{ DT} (yy ⊗⊗_{ DT} zz))
  (dα x y z xx yy zz): is_z_iso_disp
  (make_z_iso'
     (pr1 (z_iso_from_associator_iso M x y z))
     (pr2 (z_iso_from_associator_iso M x y z)))
  (dα x y z xx yy zz)
xx ⊗⊗_{ DT} (yy ⊗⊗_{ DT} zz) -->[
αinv^{ M }_{ x, y, z}] (xx ⊗⊗_{ DT} yy) ⊗⊗_{ DT} zz

    exact (pr1 aux).
  Defined.

  Definition disp_monoidal_tensor
             {C : category}
             {D : disp_cat C}
             {M : monoidal C}
             (DMD : disp_monoidal_data D M)
    : disp_tensor D M
    := pr1 DMD.

  Coercion disp_monoidal_tensor : disp_monoidal_data >-> disp_tensor.

  Definition disp_monoidal_unit
             {C : category}
             {D : disp_cat C}
             {M : monoidal C}
             (DMD : disp_monoidal_data D M)
    : D I_{M}
    := pr12 DMD.

  Notation "dI_{ DMD }" := (disp_monoidal_unit DMD).

  Definition disp_monoidal_leftunitor
             {C : category}
             {D : disp_cat C}
             {M : monoidal C}
             (DMD : disp_monoidal_data D M)
    : disp_leftunitor_data DMD dI_{DMD}
    := pr122 DMD.

  Notation "dlu_{ DMD }" := (disp_monoidal_leftunitor DMD).

  Definition disp_monoidal_leftunitorinv
             {C : category}
             {D : disp_cat C}
             {M : monoidal C}
             (DMD : disp_monoidal_data D M)
    : disp_leftunitorinv_data DMD dI_{DMD}
    := pr1 (pr222 DMD).

  Notation "dluinv_{ DMD }" := (disp_monoidal_leftunitorinv DMD).

  Definition disp_monoidal_rightunitor
             {C : category}
             {D : disp_cat C}
             {M : monoidal C}
             (DMD : disp_monoidal_data D M)
    : disp_rightunitor_data DMD dI_{DMD}
    := pr12 (pr222 DMD).

  Notation "dru_{ DMD }" := (disp_monoidal_rightunitor DMD).

  Definition disp_monoidal_rightunitorinv
             {C : category}
             {D : disp_cat C}
             {M : monoidal C}
             (DMD : disp_monoidal_data D M)
    : disp_rightunitorinv_data DMD dI_{DMD}
    := pr122 (pr222 DMD).

  Notation "druinv_{ DMD }" := (disp_monoidal_rightunitorinv DMD).

  Definition disp_monoidal_associator
             {C : category}
             {D : disp_cat C}
             {M : monoidal C}
             (DMD : disp_monoidal_data D M)
    : disp_associator_data DMD
    := pr1 (pr222 (pr222 DMD)).

  Notation "dα_{ DMD }" := (disp_monoidal_associator DMD).

  Definition disp_monoidal_associatorinv
             {C : category}
             {D : disp_cat C}
             {M : monoidal C}
             (DMD : disp_monoidal_data D M)
    : disp_associatorinv_data DMD
    := pr2 (pr222 (pr222 DMD)).

  Notation "dαinv_{ DMD }" := (disp_monoidal_associatorinv DMD).

  (** PROPERTIES **)

  Definition disp_leftunitor_nat
             {C : category}
             {D : disp_cat C}
             {M : monoidal C}
             {DT : disp_tensor D M}
             {i : D I_{M}}
             (dlu : disp_leftunitor_data DT i)
    : UU
    := ∏ (x y : C)
         (f : C⟦x,y⟧)
         (xx : D x) (yy : D y)
         (ff : xx -->[f] yy),
       (i ⊗⊗^{DT}_{l} ff) ;; (dlu y yy)
       =
       transportb
         _
         (pr1 (monoidal_leftunitorlaw M) _ _ _)
         (dlu x xx ;; ff).

  Definition disp_leftunitor_iso
             {C : category}
             {D : disp_cat C}
             {M : monoidal C}
             {DT : disp_tensor D M}
             {i : D I_{M}}
             (dlu : disp_leftunitor_data DT i)
             (dluinv : disp_leftunitorinv_data DT i)
    : UU
    := ∏ (x : C) (xx : D x),
       is_disp_inverse
         (pr2 (monoidal_leftunitorlaw M) x)
         (dlu x xx)
         (dluinv x xx).

  Definition disp_leftunitor_law
             {C : category}
             {D : disp_cat C}
             {M : monoidal C}
             {DT : disp_tensor D M}
             {i : D I_{M}}
             (dlu : disp_leftunitor_data DT i)
             (dluinv : disp_leftunitorinv_data DT i)
    : UU
    := disp_leftunitor_nat dlu × disp_leftunitor_iso dlu dluinv.

  Definition disp_leftunitorlaw_nat
             {C : category}
             {D : disp_cat C}
             {M : monoidal C}
             {DT : disp_tensor D M}
             {i : D I_{M}}
             {dlu : disp_leftunitor_data DT i}
             {dluinv : disp_leftunitorinv_data DT i}
             (dlun : disp_leftunitor_law dlu dluinv)
    : disp_leftunitor_nat dlu
    := pr1 dlun.

  Definition disp_leftunitorlaw_iso
             {C : category}
             {D : disp_cat C}
             {M : monoidal C}
             {DT : disp_tensor D M}
             {i : D I_{M}}
             {dlu : disp_leftunitor_data DT i}
             {dluinv : disp_leftunitorinv_data DT i}
             (dlui : disp_leftunitor_law dlu dluinv)
    : disp_leftunitor_iso dlu dluinv
    := pr2 dlui.

  Definition disp_rightunitor_nat
             {C : category}
             {D : disp_cat C}
             {M : monoidal C}
             {DT : disp_tensor D M}
             {i : D I_{M}}
             (dru : disp_rightunitor_data DT i)
    : UU
    := ∏ (x y : C)
         (f : C⟦x,y⟧)
         (xx : D x) (yy : D y)
         (ff : xx -->[f] yy),
       (ff ⊗⊗^{DT}_{r} i) ;; (dru y yy)
       =
       transportb
         _
         (pr1 (monoidal_rightunitorlaw M) _ _ _)
         (dru x xx ;; ff).

  Definition disp_rightunitor_iso
             {C : category}
             {D : disp_cat C}
             {M : monoidal C}
             {DT : disp_tensor D M}
             {i : D I_{M}}
             (dru : disp_rightunitor_data DT i)
             (druinv : disp_rightunitorinv_data DT i)
    : UU
    := ∏ (x : C) (xx : D x),
       is_disp_inverse
         (pr2 (monoidal_rightunitorlaw M) x)
         (dru x xx)
         (druinv x xx).

  Definition disp_rightunitor_law
             {C : category}
             {D : disp_cat C}
             {M : monoidal C}
             {DT : disp_tensor D M}
             {i : D I_{M}}
             (dru : disp_rightunitor_data DT i)
             (druinv : disp_rightunitorinv_data DT i)
    : UU
    := disp_rightunitor_nat dru × disp_rightunitor_iso dru druinv.

  Definition disp_rightunitorlaw_nat
             {C : category}
             {D : disp_cat C}
             {M : monoidal C}
             {DT : disp_tensor D M}
             {i : D I_{M}}
             {dru : disp_rightunitor_data DT i}
             {druinv : disp_rightunitorinv_data DT i}
             (drun : disp_rightunitor_law dru druinv)
    : disp_rightunitor_nat dru
    := pr1 drun.

  Definition disp_rightunitorlaw_iso
             {C : category}
             {D : disp_cat C}
             {M : monoidal C}
             {DT : disp_tensor D M}
             {i : D I_{M}}
             {dru : disp_rightunitor_data DT i}
             {druinv : disp_rightunitorinv_data DT i}
             (drui : disp_rightunitor_law dru druinv)
    : disp_rightunitor_iso dru druinv
    := pr2 drui.

  Definition disp_associator_nat_leftwhisker
             {C : category}
             {D : disp_cat C}
             {M : monoidal C}
             {DT : disp_tensor D M}
             (dα : disp_associator_data DT)
    : UU
    := ∏ (x y z1 z2 : C)
         (h : C⟦z1,z2⟧)
         (xx : D x)
         (yy : D y)
         (zz1 : D z1)
         (zz2 : D z2)
         (hh : zz1-->[h] zz2),
       (dα _ _ _ xx yy zz1) ;; (xx ⊗⊗^{DT}_{l} (yy ⊗⊗^{DT}_{l} hh))
       =
       transportb
         _
         ((associatorlaw_natleft (monoidal_associatorlaw M)) x y z1 z2 h)
         (((xx ⊗⊗_{DT} yy) ⊗⊗^{DT}_{l} hh) ;; (dα _ _ _ xx yy zz2)).

  Definition disp_associator_nat_rightwhisker
             {C : category}
             {D : disp_cat C}
             {M : monoidal C}
             {DT : disp_tensor D M}
             (dα : disp_associator_data DT)
    : UU
    := ∏ (x1 x2 y z : C)
         (f : C⟦x1,x2⟧)
         (xx1 : D x1) (xx2 : D x2) (yy : D y) (zz : D z)
         (ff : xx1-->[f] xx2),
       (dα _ _ _ xx1 yy zz) ;; (ff ⊗⊗^{DT}_{r} (yy ⊗⊗_{DT} zz))
       =
       transportb
         _
         ((associatorlaw_natright (monoidal_associatorlaw M)) x1 x2 y z f)
         (((ff ⊗⊗^{DT}_{r} yy) ⊗⊗^{DT}_{r} zz) ;; (dα _ _ _ xx2 yy zz)).

  Definition disp_associator_nat_leftrightwhisker
             {C : category}
             {D : disp_cat C}
             {M : monoidal C}
             {DT : disp_tensor D M}
             (dα : disp_associator_data DT)
    : UU
    := ∏ (x y1 y2 z : C)
         (g : C⟦y1,y2⟧)
         (xx : D x) (yy1 : D y1) (yy2 : D y2) (zz : D z)
         (gg : yy1-->[g] yy2),
       (dα _ _ _ xx yy1 zz) ;; (xx ⊗⊗^{DT}_{l} (gg ⊗⊗^{DT}_{r} zz))
       =
       transportb
         _
         ((associatorlaw_natleftright (monoidal_associatorlaw M)) x y1 y2 z g)
         (((xx ⊗⊗^{DT}_{l} gg) ⊗⊗^{DT}_{r} zz) ;; (dα _ _ _ xx yy2 zz)).

  
C: category
D: disp_cat C
M: monoidal C
DT: disp_tensor D M
dα: disp_associator_data DT
dtl: disp_associator_nat_leftwhisker dα
dtr: disp_associator_nat_rightwhisker dα
dtlr: disp_associator_nat_leftrightwhisker dα
∏ (x1 x2 y1 y2 z1 z2 : C) (xx1 : D x1) (xx2 : D x2)
(yy1 : D y1) (yy2 : D y2) (zz1 : D z1) (zz2 : D z2)
(f : C ⟦ x1, x2 ⟧) (g : C ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧)
(h : C ⟦ z1, z2 ⟧) (ff : xx1 -->[ f] xx2)
(gg : yy1 -->[ g] yy2) (hh : zz1 -->[ h] zz2),
dα x1 y1 z1 xx1 yy1 zz1 ;; ff
                           ⊗⊗^{ DT} (gg ⊗⊗^{ DT} hh) =
transportb
  (mor_disp ((xx1 ⊗⊗_{ DT} yy1) ⊗⊗_{ DT} zz1)
     (xx2 ⊗⊗_{ DT} (yy2 ⊗⊗_{ DT} zz2)))
  (associator_nat2 M f g h)
  ((ff ⊗⊗^{ DT} gg) ⊗⊗^{ DT} hh ;; dα x2 y2 z2 xx2 yy2
                                     zz2)

C: category
D: disp_cat C
M: monoidal C
DT: disp_tensor D M
dα: disp_associator_data DT
dtl: disp_associator_nat_leftwhisker dα
dtr: disp_associator_nat_rightwhisker dα
dtlr: disp_associator_nat_leftrightwhisker dα
x1, x2, y1, y2, z1, z2: C
xx1: D x1
xx2: D x2
yy1: D y1
yy2: D y2
zz1: D z1
zz2: D z2
f: C ⟦ x1, x2 ⟧
g: C ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧
h: C ⟦ z1, z2 ⟧
ff: xx1 -->[ f] xx2
gg: yy1 -->[ g] yy2
hh: zz1 -->[ h] zz2
transportb
  (mor_disp ((xx1 ⊗⊗_{ DT} yy1) ⊗⊗_{ DT} zz1)
     (xx2 ⊗⊗_{ DT} (yy2 ⊗⊗_{ DT} zz2)))
  (assoc α^{ M }_{ x1, y1, z1}
     (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M
        (bifunctor_on_objects M y1 z1) x1 x2 f)
     (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M x2
        (bifunctor_on_objects M y1 z1)
        (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z2)
        (functoronmorphisms1 M g h)))
  (transportf
     (mor_disp
        (pr1 DT (bifunctor_on_objects M x1 y1) z1
           (pr1 DT x1 y1 xx1 yy1) zz1)
        (xx2 ⊗⊗_{ DT} (yy2 ⊗⊗_{ DT} zz2)))
     (cancel_postcomposition
        (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M z1
           (bifunctor_on_objects M x1 y1)
           (bifunctor_on_objects M x2 y1)
           (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M y1 x1 x2 f)
         · α^{ M }_{ x2, y1, z1})
        (α^{ M }_{ x1, y1, z1}
         · rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M
             (bifunctor_on_objects M y1 z1) x1 x2 f)
        (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M x2
           (bifunctor_on_objects M y1 z1)
           (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z2)
           (functoronmorphisms1 M g h))
        (! associatorlaw_natright
             (monoidal_associatorlaw M) x1 x2 y1 z1 f))
     ((ff ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{r} yy1) ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{r} zz1 ;; dα x2
                                                 y1 z1
                                                 xx2
                                                 yy1
                                                 zz1 ;; 
      xx2
      ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{l} (gg ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{r} zz1 ;; yy2
                                           ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{l} hh))) =
transportb
  (mor_disp ((xx1 ⊗⊗_{ DT} yy1) ⊗⊗_{ DT} zz1)
     (xx2 ⊗⊗_{ DT} (yy2 ⊗⊗_{ DT} zz2)))
  (associator_nat2 M f g h)
  ((ff ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{r} yy1 ;; xx2 ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{l} gg)
   ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{r} zz1 ;; (xx2 ⊗⊗_{ DT} yy2)
                       ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{l} hh ;; dα x2 y2 z2
                                            xx2 yy2
                                            zz2)

    
C: category
D: disp_cat C
M: monoidal C
DT: disp_tensor D M
dα: disp_associator_data DT
dtl: disp_associator_nat_leftwhisker dα
dtr: disp_associator_nat_rightwhisker dα
dtlr: disp_associator_nat_leftrightwhisker dα
x1, x2, y1, y2, z1, z2: C
xx1: D x1
xx2: D x2
yy1: D y1
yy2: D y2
zz1: D z1
zz2: D z2
f: C ⟦ x1, x2 ⟧
g: C ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧
h: C ⟦ z1, z2 ⟧
ff: xx1 -->[ f] xx2
gg: yy1 -->[ g] yy2
hh: zz1 -->[ h] zz2
transportf
  (mor_disp
     (pr1 DT (bifunctor_on_objects M x1 y1) z1
        (pr1 DT x1 y1 xx1 yy1) zz1)
     (xx2 ⊗⊗_{ DT} (yy2 ⊗⊗_{ DT} zz2)))
  (cancel_postcomposition
     (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M z1
        (bifunctor_on_objects M x1 y1)
        (bifunctor_on_objects M x2 y1)
        (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M y1 x1 x2 f)
      · α^{ M }_{ x2, y1, z1})
     (α^{ M }_{ x1, y1, z1}
      · rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M
          (bifunctor_on_objects M y1 z1) x1 x2 f)
     (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M x2
        (bifunctor_on_objects M y1 z1)
        (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z2)
        (functoronmorphisms1 M g h))
     (! associatorlaw_natright
          (monoidal_associatorlaw M) x1 x2 y1 z1 f) @
   ! assoc α^{ M }_{ x1, y1, z1}
       (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M
          (bifunctor_on_objects M y1 z1) x1 x2 f)
       (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M x2
          (bifunctor_on_objects M y1 z1)
          (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z2)
          (functoronmorphisms1 M g h)))
  ((ff ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{r} yy1) ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{r} zz1 ;; dα x2 y1
                                               z1 xx2
                                               yy1 zz1 ;; 
   xx2
   ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{l} (gg ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{r} zz1 ;; yy2
                                        ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{l} hh)) =
transportb
  (mor_disp ((xx1 ⊗⊗_{ DT} yy1) ⊗⊗_{ DT} zz1)
     (xx2 ⊗⊗_{ DT} (yy2 ⊗⊗_{ DT} zz2)))
  (associator_nat2 M f g h)
  ((ff ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{r} yy1 ;; xx2 ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{l} gg)
   ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{r} zz1 ;; (xx2 ⊗⊗_{ DT} yy2)
                       ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{l} hh ;; dα x2 y2 z2
                                            xx2 yy2
                                            zz2)

g: C ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧
h: C ⟦ z1, z2 ⟧
ff: xx1 -->[ f] xx2
gg: yy1 -->[ g] yy2
hh: zz1 -->[ h] zz2
(ff ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{r} yy1) ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{r} zz1 ;; (dα x2 y1 z1
                                             xx2 yy1
                                             zz1 ;; 
                                           xx2
                                           ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{l} 
                                           (gg
                                            ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{r} zz1 ;; 
                                            yy2
                                            ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{l} hh)) =
transportb
  (mor_disp ((xx1 ⊗⊗_{ DT} yy1) ⊗⊗_{ DT} zz1)
     (xx2 ⊗⊗_{ DT} (yy2 ⊗⊗_{ DT} zz2)))
  ((assoc
      (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M z1
         (bifunctor_on_objects M x1 y1)
         (bifunctor_on_objects M x2 y1)
         (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M y1 x1 x2 f))
      α^{ M }_{ x2, y1, z1}
      (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M x2
         (bifunctor_on_objects M y1 z1)
         (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z2)
         (functoronmorphisms1 M g h)) @
    cancel_postcomposition
      (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M z1
         (bifunctor_on_objects M x1 y1)
         (bifunctor_on_objects M x2 y1)
         (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M y1 x1 x2 f)
       · α^{ M }_{ x2, y1, z1})
      (α^{ M }_{ x1, y1, z1}
       · rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M
           (bifunctor_on_objects M y1 z1) x1 x2 f)
      (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M x2
         (bifunctor_on_objects M y1 z1)
         (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z2)
         (functoronmorphisms1 M g h))
      (! associatorlaw_natright
           (monoidal_associatorlaw M) x1 x2 y1 z1 f) @
    ! assoc α^{ M }_{ x1, y1, z1}
        (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M
           (bifunctor_on_objects M y1 z1) x1 x2 f)
        (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M x2
           (bifunctor_on_objects M y1 z1)
           (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z2)
           (functoronmorphisms1 M g h))) @
   associator_nat2 M f g h)
  ((ff ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{r} yy1 ;; xx2 ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{l} gg)
   ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{r} zz1 ;; (xx2 ⊗⊗_{ DT} yy2)
                       ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{l} hh ;; dα x2 y2 z2
                                            xx2 yy2
                                            zz2)

zz1: D z1
zz2: D z2
f: C ⟦ x1, x2 ⟧
g: C ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧
h: C ⟦ z1, z2 ⟧
ff: xx1 -->[ f] xx2
gg: yy1 -->[ g] yy2
hh: zz1 -->[ h] zz2
(ff ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{r} yy1) ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{r} zz1 ;; transportf
                                            (mor_disp
                                               (pr1 DT
                                                 (bifunctor_on_objects
                                                 M x2
                                                 y1)
                                                 z1
                                                 (pr1
                                                 DT x2
                                                 y1
                                                 xx2
                                                 yy1)
                                                 zz1)
                                               (pr1 DT
                                                 x2
                                                 (bifunctor_on_objects
                                                 M y2
                                                 z2)
                                                 xx2
                                                 (pr1
                                                 DT y2
                                                 z2
                                                 yy2
                                                 zz2)))
                                            (maponpaths
                                               (compose
                                                 α^{ M
                                                 }_{ x2,
                                                 y1,
                                                 z1})
                                               (! 
                                                bifunctor_leftcomp
                                                 M x2
                                                 (bifunctor_on_objects
                                                 M y1
                                                 z1)
                                                 (bifunctor_on_objects
                                                 M y2
                                                 z1)
                                                 (bifunctor_on_objects
                                                 M y2
                                                 z2)
                                                 (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms
                                                 M z1
                                                 y1 y2
                                                 g)
                                                 (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms
                                                 M y2
                                                 z1 z2
                                                 h)))
                                            (dα x2 y1
                                               z1 xx2
                                               yy1 zz1 ;; 
                                             (xx2
                                              ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{l} 
                                              (gg
                                               ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{r} zz1) ;; 
                                              xx2
                                              ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{l} 
                                              (yy2
                                               ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{l} hh))) =
transportb
  (mor_disp ((xx1 ⊗⊗_{ DT} yy1) ⊗⊗_{ DT} zz1)
     (xx2 ⊗⊗_{ DT} (yy2 ⊗⊗_{ DT} zz2)))
  ((assoc
      (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M z1
         (bifunctor_on_objects M x1 y1)
         (bifunctor_on_objects M x2 y1)
         (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M y1 x1 x2 f))
      α^{ M }_{ x2, y1, z1}
      (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M x2
         (bifunctor_on_objects M y1 z1)
         (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z2)
         (functoronmorphisms1 M g h)) @
    cancel_postcomposition
      (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M z1
         (bifunctor_on_objects M x1 y1)
         (bifunctor_on_objects M x2 y1)
         (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M y1 x1 x2 f)
       · α^{ M }_{ x2, y1, z1})
      (α^{ M }_{ x1, y1, z1}
       · rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M
           (bifunctor_on_objects M y1 z1) x1 x2 f)
      (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M x2
         (bifunctor_on_objects M y1 z1)
         (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z2)
         (functoronmorphisms1 M g h))
      (! associatorlaw_natright
           (monoidal_associatorlaw M) x1 x2 y1 z1 f) @
    ! assoc α^{ M }_{ x1, y1, z1}
        (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M
           (bifunctor_on_objects M y1 z1) x1 x2 f)
        (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M x2
           (bifunctor_on_objects M y1 z1)
           (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z2)
           (functoronmorphisms1 M g h))) @
   associator_nat2 M f g h)
  ((ff ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{r} yy1 ;; xx2 ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{l} gg)
   ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{r} zz1 ;; (xx2 ⊗⊗_{ DT} yy2)
                       ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{l} hh ;; dα x2 y2 z2
                                            xx2 yy2
                                            zz2)

           (monoidal_associatorlaw M) x1 x2 y1 z1 f) @
    ! assoc α^{ M }_{ x1, y1, z1}
        (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M
           (bifunctor_on_objects M y1 z1) x1 x2 f)
        (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M x2
           (bifunctor_on_objects M y1 z1)
           (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z2)
           (functoronmorphisms1 M g h))) @
   associator_nat2 M f g h)
  ((ff ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{r} yy1 ;; xx2 ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{l} gg)
   ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{r} zz1 ;; (xx2 ⊗⊗_{ DT} yy2)
                       ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{l} hh ;; dα x2 y2 z2
                                            xx2 yy2
                                            zz2)

C: category
D: disp_cat C
M: monoidal C
DT: disp_tensor D M
dα: disp_associator_data DT
dtl: disp_associator_nat_leftwhisker dα
dtr: disp_associator_nat_rightwhisker dα
dtlr: disp_associator_nat_leftrightwhisker dα
x1, x2, y1, y2, z1, z2: C
xx1: D x1
xx2: D x2
yy1: D y1
yy2: D y2
zz1: D z1
zz2: D z2
f: C ⟦ x1, x2 ⟧
g: C ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧
h: C ⟦ z1, z2 ⟧
ff: xx1 -->[ f] xx2
gg: yy1 -->[ g] yy2
hh: zz1 -->[ h] zz2
?b =
transportb
  (mor_disp ((xx1 ⊗⊗_{ DT} yy1) ⊗⊗_{ DT} zz1)
     (xx2 ⊗⊗_{ DT} (yy2 ⊗⊗_{ DT} zz2)))
  ((assoc
      (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M z1
         (bifunctor_on_objects M x1 y1)
         (bifunctor_on_objects M x2 y1)
         (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M y1 x1 x2 f))
      α^{ M }_{ x2, y1, z1}
      (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M x2
         (bifunctor_on_objects M y1 z1)
         (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z2)
         (functoronmorphisms1 M g h)) @
    cancel_postcomposition
      (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M z1
         (bifunctor_on_objects M x1 y1)
         (bifunctor_on_objects M x2 y1)
         (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M y1 x1 x2 f)
       · α^{ M }_{ x2, y1, z1})
      (α^{ M }_{ x1, y1, z1}
       · rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M
           (bifunctor_on_objects M y1 z1) x1 x2 f)
      (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M x2
         (bifunctor_on_objects M y1 z1)
         (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z2)
         (functoronmorphisms1 M g h))
      (! associatorlaw_natright
           (monoidal_associatorlaw M) x1 x2 y1 z1 f) @
    ! assoc α^{ M }_{ x1, y1, z1}
        (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M
           (bifunctor_on_objects M y1 z1) x1 x2 f)
        (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M x2
           (bifunctor_on_objects M y1 z1)
           (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z2)
           (functoronmorphisms1 M g h))) @
   associator_nat2 M f g h)
  ((ff ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{r} yy1 ;; xx2 ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{l} gg)
   ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{r} zz1 ;; (xx2 ⊗⊗_{ DT} yy2)
                       ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{l} hh ;; 
   dα x2 y2 z2 xx2 yy2 zz2)

C: category
D: disp_cat C
M: monoidal C
DT: disp_tensor D M
dα: disp_associator_data DT
dtl: disp_associator_nat_leftwhisker dα
dtr: disp_associator_nat_rightwhisker dα
dtlr: disp_associator_nat_leftrightwhisker dα
x1, x2, y1, y2, z1, z2: C
xx1: D x1
xx2: D x2
yy1: D y1
yy2: D y2
zz1: D z1
zz2: D z2
f: C ⟦ x1, x2 ⟧
g: C ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧
h: C ⟦ z1, z2 ⟧
ff: xx1 -->[ f] xx2
gg: yy1 -->[ g] yy2
hh: zz1 -->[ h] zz2
transportf
  (mor_disp
     (pr1 DT (bifunctor_on_objects M x2 y1) z1
        (pr1 DT x2 y1 xx2 yy1) zz1)
     (pr1 DT x2 (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z2) xx2
        (pr1 DT y2 z2 yy2 zz2)))
  (! assoc α^{ M }_{ x2, y1, z1}
       (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M x2
          (bifunctor_on_objects M y1 z1)
          (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z1)
          (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M z1 y1 y2 g))
       (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M x2
          (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z1)
          (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z2)
          (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M y2 z1 z2 h)) @
   maponpaths (compose α^{ M }_{ x2, y1, z1})
     (! bifunctor_leftcomp M x2
          (bifunctor_on_objects M y1 z1)
          (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z1)
          (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z2)
          (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M z1 y1 y2 g)
          (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M y2 z1 z2 h)))
  (transportb
     (mor_disp
        (pr1 DT (bifunctor_on_objects M x2 y1) z1
           (pr1 DT x2 y1 xx2 yy1) zz1)
        (xx2 ⊗⊗_{ DT} (yy2 ⊗⊗_{ DT} zz1)))
     (associatorlaw_natleftright
        (monoidal_associatorlaw M) x2 y1 y2 z1 g)
     ((xx2 ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{l} gg) ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{r} zz1 ;; dα x2
                                                 y2 z1
                                                 xx2
                                                 yy2
                                                 zz1) ;; 
   xx2 ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{l} (yy2 ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{l} hh)) = ?t2

                                                 z1)
                                                 (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms
                                                 M z1
                                                 y1 y2
                                                 g))
                                                 (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms
                                                 M x2
                                                 (bifunctor_on_objects
                                                 M y2
                                                 z1)
                                                 (bifunctor_on_objects
                                                 M y2
                                                 z2)
                                                 (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms
                                                 M y2
                                                 z1 z2
                                                 h)) @
                                             maponpaths
                                               (compose
                                                 α^{ M
                                                 }_{ x2,
                                                 y1,
                                                 z1})
                                               (! 
                                                bifunctor_leftcomp
                                                 M x2
                                                 (bifunctor_on_objects
                                                 M y1
                                                 z1)
                                                 (bifunctor_on_objects
                                                 M y2
                                                 z1)
                                                 (bifunctor_on_objects
                                                 M y2
                                                 z2)
                                                 (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms
                                                 M z1
                                                 y1 y2
                                                 g)
                                                 (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms
                                                 M y2
                                                 z1 z2
                                                 h)))
                                            (transportf
                                               (mor_disp
                                                 (pr1
                                                 DT
                                                 (bifunctor_on_objects
                                                 M x2
                                                 y1)
                                                 z1
                                                 (pr1
                                                 DT x2
                                                 y1
                                                 xx2
                                                 yy1)
                                                 zz1)
                                                 (pr1
                                                 DT x2
                                                 (bifunctor_on_objects
                                                 M y2
                                                 z2)
                                                 xx2
                                                 (pr1
                                                 DT y2
                                                 z2
                                                 yy2
                                                 zz2)))
                                               (cancel_postcomposition
                                                 (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms
                                                 M z1
                                                 (bifunctor_on_objects
                                                 M x2
                                                 y1)
                                                 (bifunctor_on_objects
                                                 M x2
                                                 y2)

                                                 M x2
                                                 y1 y2
                                                 g)

                                                 z1})

                                                 yy2

                                                 ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{l} hh))) =

C: category
D: disp_cat C
M: monoidal C
DT: disp_tensor D M
dα: disp_associator_data DT
dtl: disp_associator_nat_leftwhisker dα
dtr: disp_associator_nat_rightwhisker dα
dtlr: disp_associator_nat_leftrightwhisker dα
x1, x2, y1, y2, z1, z2: C
xx1: D x1
xx2: D x2
yy1: D y1
yy2: D y2
zz1: D z1
zz2: D z2
f: C ⟦ x1, x2 ⟧
g: C ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧
h: C ⟦ z1, z2 ⟧
ff: xx1 -->[ f] xx2
gg: yy1 -->[ g] yy2
hh: zz1 -->[ h] zz2
?b =
transportb
  (mor_disp ((xx1 ⊗⊗_{ DT} yy1) ⊗⊗_{ DT} zz1)
     (xx2 ⊗⊗_{ DT} (yy2 ⊗⊗_{ DT} zz2)))
  ((assoc
      (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M z1
         (bifunctor_on_objects M x1 y1)
         (bifunctor_on_objects M x2 y1)
         (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M y1 x1 x2 f))
      α^{ M }_{ x2, y1, z1}
      (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M x2
         (bifunctor_on_objects M y1 z1)
         (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z2)
         (functoronmorphisms1 M g h)) @
    cancel_postcomposition
      (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M z1
         (bifunctor_on_objects M x1 y1)
         (bifunctor_on_objects M x2 y1)
         (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M y1 x1 x2 f)
       · α^{ M }_{ x2, y1, z1})
      (α^{ M }_{ x1, y1, z1}
       · rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M
           (bifunctor_on_objects M y1 z1) x1 x2 f)
      (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M x2
         (bifunctor_on_objects M y1 z1)
         (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z2)
         (functoronmorphisms1 M g h))
      (! associatorlaw_natright
           (monoidal_associatorlaw M) x1 x2 y1 z1 f) @
    ! assoc α^{ M }_{ x1, y1, z1}
        (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M
           (bifunctor_on_objects M y1 z1) x1 x2 f)
        (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M x2
           (bifunctor_on_objects M y1 z1)
           (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z2)
           (functoronmorphisms1 M g h))) @
   associator_nat2 M f g h)
  ((ff ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{r} yy1 ;; xx2 ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{l} gg)
   ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{r} zz1 ;; (xx2 ⊗⊗_{ DT} yy2)
                       ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{l} hh ;; 
   dα x2 y2 z2 xx2 yy2 zz2)

C: category
D: disp_cat C
M: monoidal C
DT: disp_tensor D M
dα: disp_associator_data DT
dtl: disp_associator_nat_leftwhisker dα
dtr: disp_associator_nat_rightwhisker dα
dtlr: disp_associator_nat_leftrightwhisker dα
x1, x2, y1, y2, z1, z2: C
xx1: D x1
xx2: D x2
yy1: D y1
yy2: D y2
zz1: D z1
zz2: D z2
f: C ⟦ x1, x2 ⟧
g: C ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧
h: C ⟦ z1, z2 ⟧
ff: xx1 -->[ f] xx2
gg: yy1 -->[ g] yy2
hh: zz1 -->[ h] zz2
transportf
  (mor_disp
     (pr1 DT (bifunctor_on_objects M x2 y1) z1
        (pr1 DT x2 y1 xx2 yy1) zz1)
     (pr1 DT x2 (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z2) xx2
        (pr1 DT y2 z2 yy2 zz2)))
  (! assoc α^{ M }_{ x2, y1, z1}
       (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M x2
          (bifunctor_on_objects M y1 z1)
          (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z1)
          (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M z1 y1 y2 g))
       (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M x2
          (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z1)
          (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z2)
          (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M y2 z1 z2 h)) @
   maponpaths (compose α^{ M }_{ x2, y1, z1})
     (! bifunctor_leftcomp M x2
          (bifunctor_on_objects M y1 z1)
          (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z1)
          (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z2)
          (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M z1 y1 y2 g)
          (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M y2 z1 z2 h)))
  (transportf
     (mor_disp
        (pr1 DT (bifunctor_on_objects M x2 y1) z1
           (pr1 DT x2 y1 xx2 yy1) zz1)
        (pr1 DT x2 (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z2) xx2
           (pr1 DT y2 z2 yy2 zz2)))
     (cancel_postcomposition
        (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M z1
           (bifunctor_on_objects M x2 y1)
           (bifunctor_on_objects M x2 y2)
           (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M x2 y1 y2 g)
         · α^{ M }_{ x2, y2, z1})
        (α^{ M }_{ x2, y1, z1}
         · leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M x2
             (bifunctor_on_objects M y1 z1)
             (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z1)
             (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M z1 y1 y2
                g))
        (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M x2
           (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z1)
           (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z2)
           (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M y2 z1 z2 h))
        (! associatorlaw_natleftright
             (monoidal_associatorlaw M) x2 y1 y2 z1 g))
     ((xx2 ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{l} gg) ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{r} zz1 ;; dα x2
                                                 y2 z1
                                                 xx2
                                                 yy2
                                                 zz1 ;; 
      xx2 ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{l} (yy2 ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{l} hh))) = ?t2

      apply transport_f_f.

                                                 M) x2
                                                 y1 y2
                                                 z1 g) @
                                             ! assoc
                                                 α^{ M
                                                 }_{ x2,
                                                 y1,
                                                 z1}

                                                 M x2

                                              ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{l} hh)) =

C: category
D: disp_cat C
M: monoidal C
DT: disp_tensor D M
dα: disp_associator_data DT
dtl: disp_associator_nat_leftwhisker dα
dtr: disp_associator_nat_rightwhisker dα
dtlr: disp_associator_nat_leftrightwhisker dα
x1, x2, y1, y2, z1, z2: C
xx1: D x1
xx2: D x2
yy1: D y1
yy2: D y2
zz1: D z1
zz2: D z2
f: C ⟦ x1, x2 ⟧
g: C ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧
h: C ⟦ z1, z2 ⟧
ff: xx1 -->[ f] xx2
gg: yy1 -->[ g] yy2
hh: zz1 -->[ h] zz2
?b =
transportb
  (mor_disp ((xx1 ⊗⊗_{ DT} yy1) ⊗⊗_{ DT} zz1)
     (xx2 ⊗⊗_{ DT} (yy2 ⊗⊗_{ DT} zz2)))
  ((assoc
      (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M z1
         (bifunctor_on_objects M x1 y1)
         (bifunctor_on_objects M x2 y1)
         (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M y1 x1 x2 f))
      α^{ M }_{ x2, y1, z1}
      (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M x2
         (bifunctor_on_objects M y1 z1)
         (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z2)
         (functoronmorphisms1 M g h)) @
    cancel_postcomposition
      (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M z1
         (bifunctor_on_objects M x1 y1)
         (bifunctor_on_objects M x2 y1)
         (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M y1 x1 x2 f)
       · α^{ M }_{ x2, y1, z1})
      (α^{ M }_{ x1, y1, z1}
       · rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M
           (bifunctor_on_objects M y1 z1) x1 x2 f)
      (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M x2
         (bifunctor_on_objects M y1 z1)
         (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z2)
         (functoronmorphisms1 M g h))
      (! associatorlaw_natright
           (monoidal_associatorlaw M) x1 x2 y1 z1 f) @
    ! assoc α^{ M }_{ x1, y1, z1}
        (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M
           (bifunctor_on_objects M y1 z1) x1 x2 f)
        (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M x2
           (bifunctor_on_objects M y1 z1)
           (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z2)
           (functoronmorphisms1 M g h))) @
   associator_nat2 M f g h)
  ((ff ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{r} yy1 ;; xx2 ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{l} gg)
   ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{r} zz1 ;; (xx2 ⊗⊗_{ DT} yy2)
                       ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{l} hh ;; 
   dα x2 y2 z2 xx2 yy2 zz2)

C: category
D: disp_cat C
M: monoidal C
DT: disp_tensor D M
dα: disp_associator_data DT
dtl: disp_associator_nat_leftwhisker dα
dtr: disp_associator_nat_rightwhisker dα
dtlr: disp_associator_nat_leftrightwhisker dα

xx2: D x2

yy2: D y2

zz2: D z2

transportf
  (mor_disp ((xx1 ⊗⊗_{ DT} yy1) ⊗⊗_{ DT} zz1)
     (pr1 DT x2 (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z2) xx2
        (pr1 DT y2 z2 yy2 zz2)))
  (maponpaths
     (compose
        (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M z1
           (bifunctor_on_objects M x1 y1)
           (bifunctor_on_objects M x2 y1)
           (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M y1 x1 x2 f)))
     (cancel_postcomposition
        (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M z1
           (bifunctor_on_objects M x2 y1)
           (bifunctor_on_objects M x2 y2)
           (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M x2 y1 y2 g)
         · α^{ M }_{ x2, y2, z1})
        (α^{ M }_{ x2, y1, z1}
         · leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M x2
             (bifunctor_on_objects M y1 z1)
             (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z1)
             (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M z1 y1 y2
                g))
        (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M x2
           (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z1)
           (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z2)

             (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z1)
             (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M z1 y1 y2
                g))
          (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M x2
             (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z1)
             (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z2)
             (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M y2 z1 z2 h)) @
      maponpaths (compose α^{ M }_{ x2, y1, z1})
        (! bifunctor_leftcomp M x2
             (bifunctor_on_objects M y1 z1)
             (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z1)
             (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z2)
             (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M z1 y1 y2
                g)
             (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M y2 z1 z2 h))))
  ((ff ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{r} yy1) ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{r} zz1 ;; ((xx2

             (bifunctor_on_objects M y1 z1)

             (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M z1 y1 y2
                g))
          (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M x2
             (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z1)
             (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z2)
             (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M y2 z1 z2 h)) @
      maponpaths (compose α^{ M }_{ x2, y1, z1})
        (! bifunctor_leftcomp M x2
             (bifunctor_on_objects M y1 z1)
             (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z1)
             (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z2)
             (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M z1 y1 y2
                g)
             (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M y2 z1 z2 h))))
  (transportb
     (mor_disp ((xx1 ⊗⊗_{ DT} yy1) ⊗⊗_{ DT} zz1)
        (xx2 ⊗⊗_{ DT} (yy2 ⊗⊗_{ DT} zz2)))
     ((assoc
         (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M z1
            (bifunctor_on_objects M x1 y1)
            (bifunctor_on_objects M x2 y1)
            (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M y1 x1 x2 f))
         α^{ M }_{ x2, y1, z1}
         (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M x2
            (bifunctor_on_objects M y1 z1)
            (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z2)
            (functoronmorphisms1 M g h)) @
       cancel_postcomposition
         (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M z1
            (bifunctor_on_objects M x1 y1)
            (bifunctor_on_objects M x2 y1)
            (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M y1 x1 x2 f)
          · α^{ M }_{ x2, y1, z1})
         (α^{ M }_{ x1, y1, z1}
          · rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M
              (bifunctor_on_objects M y1 z1) x1 x2 f)
         (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M x2
            (bifunctor_on_objects M y1 z1)
            (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z2)
            (functoronmorphisms1 M g h))
         (! associatorlaw_natright
              (monoidal_associatorlaw M) x1 x2 y1 z1 f) @
       ! assoc α^{ M }_{ x1, y1, z1}
           (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M
              (bifunctor_on_objects M y1 z1) x1 x2 f)
           (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M x2
              (bifunctor_on_objects M y1 z1)
              (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z2)
              (functoronmorphisms1 M g h))) @
      associator_nat2 M f g h)
     ((ff ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{r} yy1 ;; xx2 ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{l} gg)
      ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{r} zz1 ;; 
      (xx2 ⊗⊗_{ DT} yy2) ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{l} hh ;; 
      dα x2 y2 z2 xx2 yy2 zz2))

     (xx2 ⊗⊗_{ DT} (yy2 ⊗⊗_{ DT} zz2)))

     (compose
        (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M z1
           (bifunctor_on_objects M x1 y1)
           (bifunctor_on_objects M x2 y1)
           (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M y1 x1 x2 f)))
     (cancel_postcomposition
        (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M z1

           (bifunctor_on_objects M x2 y2)
           (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M x2 y1 y2 g)
         · α^{ M }_{ x2, y2, z1})
        (α^{ M }_{ x2, y1, z1}
         · leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M x2
             (bifunctor_on_objects M y1 z1)
             (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z1)
             (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M z1 y1 y2
                g))
        (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M x2
           (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z1)
           (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z2)
           (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M y2 z1 z2 h))
        (! associatorlaw_natleftright
             (monoidal_associatorlaw M) x2 y1 y2 z1 g) @
      ! assoc α^{ M }_{ x2, y1, z1}
          (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M x2
             (bifunctor_on_objects M y1 z1)
             (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z1)

                g))

             (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z1)
             (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z2)
             (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M y2 z1 z2 h)) @
      maponpaths (compose α^{ M }_{ x2, y1, z1})
        (! bifunctor_leftcomp M x2
             (bifunctor_on_objects M y1 z1)

             (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M y2 z1 z2 h))))

              (bifunctor_on_objects M y1 z1) x1 x2 f)
           (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M x2
              (bifunctor_on_objects M y1 z1)
              (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z2)
              (functoronmorphisms1 M g h))) @
      associator_nat2 M f g h)
     ((ff ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{r} yy1 ;; xx2 ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{l} gg)
      ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{r} zz1 ;; 
      (xx2 ⊗⊗_{ DT} yy2) ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{l} hh ;; 
      dα x2 y2 z2 xx2 yy2 zz2))

 apply mor_disp_transportf_prewhisker. 
C: category
D: disp_cat C
M: monoidal C
DT: disp_tensor D M
dα: disp_associator_data DT
dtl: disp_associator_nat_leftwhisker dα
dtr: disp_associator_nat_rightwhisker dα
dtlr: disp_associator_nat_leftrightwhisker dα
x1, x2, y1, y2, z1, z2: C
xx1: D x1
xx2: D x2
yy1: D y1
yy2: D y2
zz1: D z1
zz2: D z2
f: C ⟦ x1, x2 ⟧
g: C ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧
h: C ⟦ z1, z2 ⟧
ff: xx1 -->[ f] xx2
gg: yy1 -->[ g] yy2
hh: zz1 -->[ h] zz2
transportf
  (mor_disp ((xx1 ⊗⊗_{ DT} yy1) ⊗⊗_{ DT} zz1)
     (pr1 DT x2 (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z2) xx2
        (pr1 DT y2 z2 yy2 zz2)))
  (maponpaths
     (compose
        (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M z1
           (bifunctor_on_objects M x1 y1)
           (bifunctor_on_objects M x2 y1)
           (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M y1 x1 x2 f)))
     (assoc
        (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M z1
           (bifunctor_on_objects M x2 y1)
           (bifunctor_on_objects M x2 y2)
           (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M x2 y1 y2 g))
        α^{ M }_{ x2, y2, z1}
        (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M x2
           (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z1)
           (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z2)
           (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M y2 z1 z2 h))))
  ((ff ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{r} yy1) ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{r} zz1 ;; ((xx2
                                               ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{l} gg)
                                              ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{r} zz1 ;; 
                                              transportb
                                                (mor_disp
                                                 (pr1
                                                 DT
                                                 (bifunctor_on_objects
                                                 M x2

                                                 y2 z2

                                                 yy2
                                                 zz2))) =
transportb
  (mor_disp ((xx1 ⊗⊗_{ DT} yy1) ⊗⊗_{ DT} zz1)
     (xx2 ⊗⊗_{ DT} (yy2 ⊗⊗_{ DT} zz2)))
  (maponpaths
     (compose
        (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M z1
           (bifunctor_on_objects M x1 y1)
           (bifunctor_on_objects M x2 y1)
           (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M y1 x1 x2 f)))
     (cancel_postcomposition
        (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M z1
           (bifunctor_on_objects M x2 y1)
           (bifunctor_on_objects M x2 y2)
           (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M x2 y1 y2 g)
         · α^{ M }_{ x2, y2, z1})
        (α^{ M }_{ x2, y1, z1}
         · leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M x2
             (bifunctor_on_objects M y1 z1)
             (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z1)
             (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M z1 y1 y2
                g))
        (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M x2
           (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z1)
           (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z2)
           (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M y2 z1 z2 h))
        (! associatorlaw_natleftright
             (monoidal_associatorlaw M) x2 y1 y2 z1 g) @
      ! assoc α^{ M }_{ x2, y1, z1}
          (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M x2
             (bifunctor_on_objects M y1 z1)
             (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z1)
             (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M z1 y1 y2
                g))
          (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M x2
             (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z1)
             (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z2)
             (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M y2 z1 z2 h)) @
      maponpaths (compose α^{ M }_{ x2, y1, z1})
        (! bifunctor_leftcomp M x2
             (bifunctor_on_objects M y1 z1)
             (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z1)
             (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z2)
             (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M z1 y1 y2
                g)
             (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M y2 z1 z2 h))))
  (transportb
     (mor_disp ((xx1 ⊗⊗_{ DT} yy1) ⊗⊗_{ DT} zz1)
        (xx2 ⊗⊗_{ DT} (yy2 ⊗⊗_{ DT} zz2)))
     ((assoc
         (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M z1
            (bifunctor_on_objects M x1 y1)
            (bifunctor_on_objects M x2 y1)
            (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M y1 x1 x2 f))
         α^{ M }_{ x2, y1, z1}
         (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M x2
            (bifunctor_on_objects M y1 z1)
            (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z2)
            (functoronmorphisms1 M g h)) @
       cancel_postcomposition
         (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M z1
            (bifunctor_on_objects M x1 y1)
            (bifunctor_on_objects M x2 y1)
            (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M y1 x1 x2 f)
          · α^{ M }_{ x2, y1, z1})
         (α^{ M }_{ x1, y1, z1}
          · rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M
              (bifunctor_on_objects M y1 z1) x1 x2 f)
         (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M x2
            (bifunctor_on_objects M y1 z1)
            (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z2)
            (functoronmorphisms1 M g h))
         (! associatorlaw_natright
              (monoidal_associatorlaw M) x1 x2 y1 z1 f) @
       ! assoc α^{ M }_{ x1, y1, z1}
           (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M
              (bifunctor_on_objects M y1 z1) x1 x2 f)
           (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M x2
              (bifunctor_on_objects M y1 z1)
              (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z2)
              (functoronmorphisms1 M g h))) @
      associator_nat2 M f g h)
     ((ff ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{r} yy1 ;; xx2 ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{l} gg)
      ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{r} zz1 ;; (xx2 ⊗⊗_{ DT} yy2)
                          ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{l} hh ;; dα x2 y2
                                               z2 xx2
                                               yy2 zz2))

     (transportb
        (mor_disp ((xx1 ⊗⊗_{ DT} yy1) ⊗⊗_{ DT} zz1)
           (xx2 ⊗⊗_{ DT} (yy2 ⊗⊗_{ DT} zz2)))
        ((assoc
            (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M z1
               (bifunctor_on_objects M x1 y1)
               (bifunctor_on_objects M x2 y1)
               (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M y1 x1
                  x2 f)) 
            α^{ M }_{ x2, y1, z1}
            (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M x2
               (bifunctor_on_objects M y1 z1)
               (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z2)
               (functoronmorphisms1 M g h)) @
          cancel_postcomposition
            (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M z1
               (bifunctor_on_objects M x1 y1)
               (bifunctor_on_objects M x2 y1)
               (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M y1 x1
                  x2 f) · 
             α^{ M }_{ x2, y1, z1})
            (α^{ M }_{ x1, y1, z1}
             · rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M
                 (bifunctor_on_objects M y1 z1) x1 x2
                 f)
            (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M x2
               (bifunctor_on_objects M y1 z1)
               (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z2)
               (functoronmorphisms1 M g h))
            (! associatorlaw_natright
                 (monoidal_associatorlaw M) x1 x2 y1
                 z1 f) @
          ! assoc α^{ M }_{ x1, y1, z1}
              (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M
                 (bifunctor_on_objects M y1 z1) x1 x2
                 f)
              (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M x2
                 (bifunctor_on_objects M y1 z1)
                 (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z2)
                 (functoronmorphisms1 M g h))) @
         associator_nat2 M f g h)
        ((ff ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{r} yy1 ;; xx2 ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{l} gg)
         ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{r} zz1 ;; 
         (xx2 ⊗⊗_{ DT} yy2) ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{l} hh ;; 
         dα x2 y2 z2 xx2 yy2 zz2)))

C: category
D: disp_cat C
M: monoidal C

dα: disp_associator_data DT

transportb
  (mor_disp ((xx1 ⊗⊗_{ DT} yy1) ⊗⊗_{ DT} zz1)
     (xx2 ⊗⊗_{ DT} (yy2 ⊗⊗_{ DT} zz2)))
  (maponpaths
     (compose
        (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M z1
           (bifunctor_on_objects M x1 y1)
           (bifunctor_on_objects M x2 y1)
           (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M y1 x1 x2 f)))
     (assoc
        (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M z1
           (bifunctor_on_objects M x2 y1)
           (bifunctor_on_objects M x2 y2)
           (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M x2 y1 y2 g))
        α^{ M }_{ x2, y2, z1}
        (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M x2
           (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z1)
           (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z2)
           (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M y2 z1 z2 h))))
  (transportb
     (mor_disp ((xx1 ⊗⊗_{ DT} yy1) ⊗⊗_{ DT} zz1)
        (xx2 ⊗⊗_{ DT} (yy2 ⊗⊗_{ DT} zz2)))
     (maponpaths
        (compose
           (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M z1
              (bifunctor_on_objects M x1 y1)
              (bifunctor_on_objects M x2 y1)
              (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M y1 x1 x2
                 f)))
        (cancel_postcomposition
           (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M z1
              (bifunctor_on_objects M x2 y1)
              (bifunctor_on_objects M x2 y2)
              (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M x2 y1 y2
                 g) · α^{ M }_{ x2, y2, z1})
           (α^{ M }_{ x2, y1, z1}
            · leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M x2
                (bifunctor_on_objects M y1 z1)
                (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z1)
                (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M z1 y1
                   y2 g))
           (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M x2
              (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z1)
              (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z2)
              (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M y2 z1 z2
                 h))
           (! associatorlaw_natleftright
                (monoidal_associatorlaw M) x2 y1 y2 z1
                g) @
         ! assoc α^{ M }_{ x2, y1, z1}
             (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M x2
                (bifunctor_on_objects M y1 z1)
                (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z1)
                (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M z1 y1
                   y2 g))
             (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M x2
                (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z1)
                (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z2)
                (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M y2 z1
                   z2 h)) @
         maponpaths (compose α^{ M }_{ x2, y1, z1})
           (! bifunctor_leftcomp M x2
                (bifunctor_on_objects M y1 z1)
                (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z1)
                (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z2)
                (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M z1 y1
                   y2 g)
                (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M y2 z1
                   z2 h))))
     (transportb
        (mor_disp ((xx1 ⊗⊗_{ DT} yy1) ⊗⊗_{ DT} zz1)

        ((assoc

                  x2 f)) α^{ M }_{ x2, y1, z1}

               (bifunctor_on_objects M y1 z1)
               (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z2)
               (functoronmorphisms1 M g h)) @
          cancel_postcomposition
            (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M z1
               (bifunctor_on_objects M x1 y1)
               (bifunctor_on_objects M x2 y1)
               (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M y1 x1
                  x2 f) · α^{ M }_{ x2, y1, z1})
            (α^{ M }_{ x1, y1, z1}
             · rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M
                 (bifunctor_on_objects M y1 z1) x1 x2
                 f)
            (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M x2
               (bifunctor_on_objects M y1 z1)
               (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z2)
               (functoronmorphisms1 M g h))
            (! associatorlaw_natright
                 (monoidal_associatorlaw M) x1 x2 y1
                 z1 f) @
          ! assoc α^{ M }_{ x1, y1, z1}
              (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M

                 f)
              (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M x2
                 (bifunctor_on_objects M y1 z1)
                 (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z2)
                 (functoronmorphisms1 M g h))) @
         associator_nat2 M f g h)
        ((ff ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{r} yy1 ;; xx2 ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{l} gg)
         ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{r} zz1 ;; (xx2 ⊗⊗_{ DT} yy2)

                                                 y2 z2

                                                 zz2)))

xx2: D x2
yy1: D y1
yy2: D y2
zz1: D z1
zz2: D z2
f: C ⟦ x1, x2 ⟧
g: C ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧
h: C ⟦ z1, z2 ⟧
ff: xx1 -->[ f] xx2
gg: yy1 -->[ g] yy2
hh: zz1 -->[ h] zz2
transportf
  (mor_disp ((xx1 ⊗⊗_{ DT} yy1) ⊗⊗_{ DT} zz1)
     (xx2 ⊗⊗_{ DT} (yy2 ⊗⊗_{ DT} zz2)))
  (maponpaths
     (compose
        (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M z1
           (bifunctor_on_objects M x1 y1)
           (bifunctor_on_objects M x2 y1)
           (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M y1 x1 x2 f)))
     (maponpaths
        (compose
           (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M z1
              (bifunctor_on_objects M x2 y1)
              (bifunctor_on_objects M x2 y2)
              (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M x2 y1 y2
                 g)))
        (! associatorlaw_natleft
             (monoidal_associatorlaw M) x2 y2 z1 z2 h)))
  ((ff ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{r} yy1) ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{r} zz1 ;; ((xx2
                                               ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{l} gg)
                                              ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{r} zz1 ;; 
                                              ((xx2
                                                ⊗⊗_{ DT} yy2)
                                               ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{l} hh ;; 
                                               dα x2
                                                 y2 z2
                                                 xx2
                                                 yy2
                                                 zz2))) =
transportb
  (mor_disp ((xx1 ⊗⊗_{ DT} yy1) ⊗⊗_{ DT} zz1)
     (xx2 ⊗⊗_{ DT} (yy2 ⊗⊗_{ DT} zz2)))
  (maponpaths
     (compose
        (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M z1
           (bifunctor_on_objects M x1 y1)
           (bifunctor_on_objects M x2 y1)
           (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M y1 x1 x2 f)))
     (assoc
        (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M z1
           (bifunctor_on_objects M x2 y1)
           (bifunctor_on_objects M x2 y2)
           (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M x2 y1 y2 g))
        α^{ M }_{ x2, y2, z1}
        (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M x2
           (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z1)
           (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z2)
           (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M y2 z1 z2 h))))
  (transportb
     (mor_disp ((xx1 ⊗⊗_{ DT} yy1) ⊗⊗_{ DT} zz1)
        (xx2 ⊗⊗_{ DT} (yy2 ⊗⊗_{ DT} zz2)))
     (maponpaths
        (compose
           (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M z1
              (bifunctor_on_objects M x1 y1)
              (bifunctor_on_objects M x2 y1)
              (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M y1 x1 x2
                 f)))
        (cancel_postcomposition
           (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M z1
              (bifunctor_on_objects M x2 y1)
              (bifunctor_on_objects M x2 y2)
              (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M x2 y1 y2
                 g) · α^{ M }_{ x2, y2, z1})
           (α^{ M }_{ x2, y1, z1}
            · leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M x2
                (bifunctor_on_objects M y1 z1)
                (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z1)
                (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M z1 y1
                   y2 g))
           (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M x2
              (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z1)
              (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z2)
              (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M y2 z1 z2
                 h))
           (! associatorlaw_natleftright
                (monoidal_associatorlaw M) x2 y1 y2 z1
                g) @
         ! assoc α^{ M }_{ x2, y1, z1}
             (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M x2
                (bifunctor_on_objects M y1 z1)
                (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z1)
                (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M z1 y1
                   y2 g))
             (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M x2
                (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z1)
                (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z2)
                (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M y2 z1
                   z2 h)) @
         maponpaths (compose α^{ M }_{ x2, y1, z1})
           (! bifunctor_leftcomp M x2
                (bifunctor_on_objects M y1 z1)
                (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z1)
                (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z2)
                (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M z1 y1
                   y2 g)
                (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M y2 z1
                   z2 h))))
     (transportb
        (mor_disp ((xx1 ⊗⊗_{ DT} yy1) ⊗⊗_{ DT} zz1)
           (xx2 ⊗⊗_{ DT} (yy2 ⊗⊗_{ DT} zz2)))
        ((assoc
            (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M z1
               (bifunctor_on_objects M x1 y1)
               (bifunctor_on_objects M x2 y1)
               (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M y1 x1
                  x2 f)) α^{ M }_{ x2, y1, z1}
            (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M x2
               (bifunctor_on_objects M y1 z1)
               (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z2)
               (functoronmorphisms1 M g h)) @
          cancel_postcomposition
            (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M z1
               (bifunctor_on_objects M x1 y1)
               (bifunctor_on_objects M x2 y1)
               (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M y1 x1
                  x2 f) · α^{ M }_{ x2, y1, z1})
            (α^{ M }_{ x1, y1, z1}
             · rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M
                 (bifunctor_on_objects M y1 z1) x1 x2
                 f)
            (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M x2
               (bifunctor_on_objects M y1 z1)
               (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z2)
               (functoronmorphisms1 M g h))
            (! associatorlaw_natright
                 (monoidal_associatorlaw M) x1 x2 y1
                 z1 f) @
          ! assoc α^{ M }_{ x1, y1, z1}
              (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M
                 (bifunctor_on_objects M y1 z1) x1 x2
                 f)
              (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M x2
                 (bifunctor_on_objects M y1 z1)
                 (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z2)
                 (functoronmorphisms1 M g h))) @
         associator_nat2 M f g h)
        ((ff ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{r} yy1 ;; xx2 ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{l} gg)
         ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{r} zz1 ;; (xx2 ⊗⊗_{ DT} yy2)
                             ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{l} hh ;; dα x2
                                                 y2 z2
                                                 xx2
                                                 yy2
                                                 zz2)))

        (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M y1 x1 x2 f))
     (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M z1
        (bifunctor_on_objects M x2 y1)
        (bifunctor_on_objects M x2 y2)
        (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M x2 y1 y2 g))
     (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M
        (bifunctor_on_objects M x2 y2) z1 z2 h
      · α^{ M }_{ x2, y2, z2}))
  ((ff ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{r} yy1) ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{r} zz1 ;; (xx2
                                              ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{l} gg)
                                             ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{r} zz1 ;; 
   ((xx2 ⊗⊗_{ DT} yy2) ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{l} hh ;; dα x2 y2 z2
                                            xx2 yy2
                                            zz2)) = 
?b
C: category
D: disp_cat C
M: monoidal C
DT: disp_tensor D M
dα: disp_associator_data DT
dtl: disp_associator_nat_leftwhisker dα
dtr: disp_associator_nat_rightwhisker dα
dtlr: disp_associator_nat_leftrightwhisker dα
x1, x2, y1, y2, z1, z2: C
xx1: D x1
xx2: D x2
yy1: D y1
yy2: D y2
zz1: D z1
zz2: D z2
f: C ⟦ x1, x2 ⟧
g: C ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧
h: C ⟦ z1, z2 ⟧
ff: xx1 -->[ f] xx2
gg: yy1 -->[ g] yy2
hh: zz1 -->[ h] zz2
?b =
transportb
  (mor_disp ((xx1 ⊗⊗_{ DT} yy1) ⊗⊗_{ DT} zz1)
     (xx2 ⊗⊗_{ DT} (yy2 ⊗⊗_{ DT} zz2)))
  (maponpaths
     (compose
        (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M z1
           (bifunctor_on_objects M x1 y1)
           (bifunctor_on_objects M x2 y1)
           (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M y1 x1 x2 f)))
     (maponpaths
        (compose
           (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M z1
              (bifunctor_on_objects M x2 y1)
              (bifunctor_on_objects M x2 y2)
              (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M x2 y1 y2
                 g)))
        (! associatorlaw_natleft
             (monoidal_associatorlaw M) x2 y2 z1 z2 h)))
  (transportb
     (mor_disp ((xx1 ⊗⊗_{ DT} yy1) ⊗⊗_{ DT} zz1)
        (xx2 ⊗⊗_{ DT} (yy2 ⊗⊗_{ DT} zz2)))
     (maponpaths
        (compose
           (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M z1
              (bifunctor_on_objects M x1 y1)
              (bifunctor_on_objects M x2 y1)
              (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M y1 x1 x2
                 f)))
        (assoc
           (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M z1
              (bifunctor_on_objects M x2 y1)
              (bifunctor_on_objects M x2 y2)
              (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M x2 y1 y2
                 g)) α^{ M }_{ x2, y2, z1}
           (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M x2
              (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z1)
              (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z2)
              (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M y2 z1 z2
                 h))))
     (transportb
        (mor_disp ((xx1 ⊗⊗_{ DT} yy1) ⊗⊗_{ DT} zz1)
           (xx2 ⊗⊗_{ DT} (yy2 ⊗⊗_{ DT} zz2)))
        (maponpaths
           (compose
              (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M z1
                 (bifunctor_on_objects M x1 y1)
                 (bifunctor_on_objects M x2 y1)
                 (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M y1 x1
                    x2 f)))
           (cancel_postcomposition
              (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M z1
                 (bifunctor_on_objects M x2 y1)
                 (bifunctor_on_objects M x2 y2)
                 (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M x2 y1
                    y2 g) · 
               α^{ M }_{ x2, y2, z1})
              (α^{ M }_{ x2, y1, z1}
               · leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M x2
                   (bifunctor_on_objects M y1 z1)
                   (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z1)
                   (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M z1
                      y1 y2 g))
              (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M x2
                 (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z1)
                 (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z2)
                 (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M y2 z1
                    z2 h))
              (! associatorlaw_natleftright
                   (monoidal_associatorlaw M) x2 y1 y2
                   z1 g) @
            ! assoc α^{ M }_{ x2, y1, z1}
                (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M x2
                   (bifunctor_on_objects M y1 z1)
                   (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z1)
                   (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M z1
                      y1 y2 g))
                (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M x2
                   (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z1)
                   (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z2)
                   (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M y2
                      z1 z2 h)) @
            maponpaths (compose α^{ M }_{ x2, y1, z1})
              (! bifunctor_leftcomp M x2
                   (bifunctor_on_objects M y1 z1)
                   (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z1)
                   (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z2)
                   (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M z1
                      y1 y2 g)
                   (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M y2
                      z1 z2 h))))
        (transportb
           (mor_disp ((xx1 ⊗⊗_{ DT} yy1) ⊗⊗_{ DT} zz1)
              (xx2 ⊗⊗_{ DT} (yy2 ⊗⊗_{ DT} zz2)))
           ((assoc
               (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M z1
                  (bifunctor_on_objects M x1 y1)
                  (bifunctor_on_objects M x2 y1)
                  (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M y1
                     x1 x2 f)) 
               α^{ M }_{ x2, y1, z1}
               (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M x2
                  (bifunctor_on_objects M y1 z1)
                  (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z2)
                  (functoronmorphisms1 M g h)) @
             cancel_postcomposition
               (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M z1
                  (bifunctor_on_objects M x1 y1)
                  (bifunctor_on_objects M x2 y1)
                  (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M y1
                     x1 x2 f) · 
                α^{ M }_{ x2, y1, z1})
               (α^{ M }_{ x1, y1, z1}
                · rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M
                    (bifunctor_on_objects M y1 z1) x1
                    x2 f)
               (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M x2
                  (bifunctor_on_objects M y1 z1)
                  (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z2)
                  (functoronmorphisms1 M g h))
               (! associatorlaw_natright
                    (monoidal_associatorlaw M) x1 x2
                    y1 z1 f) @
             ! assoc α^{ M }_{ x1, y1, z1}
                 (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M
                    (bifunctor_on_objects M y1 z1) x1
                    x2 f)
                 (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M x2
                    (bifunctor_on_objects M y1 z1)
                    (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z2)
                    (functoronmorphisms1 M g h))) @
            associator_nat2 M f g h)
           ((ff ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{r} yy1 ;; 
             xx2 ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{l} gg) ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{r} zz1 ;; 
            (xx2 ⊗⊗_{ DT} yy2) ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{l} hh ;; 
            dα x2 y2 z2 xx2 yy2 zz2))))

        (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M z1
           (bifunctor_on_objects M x1 y1)
           (bifunctor_on_objects M x2 y1)
           (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M y1 x1 x2 f)))
     (maponpaths
        (compose
           (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M z1
              (bifunctor_on_objects M x2 y1)
              (bifunctor_on_objects M x2 y2)
              (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M x2 y1 y2
                 g)))
        (! associatorlaw_natleft
             (monoidal_associatorlaw M) x2 y2 z1 z2 h)) @
   maponpaths
     (compose
        (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M z1
           (bifunctor_on_objects M x1 y1)
           (bifunctor_on_objects M x2 y1)
           (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M y1 x1 x2 f)))
     (assoc
        (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M z1
           (bifunctor_on_objects M x2 y1)
           (bifunctor_on_objects M x2 y2)
           (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M x2 y1 y2 g))
        α^{ M }_{ x2, y2, z1}
        (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M x2
           (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z1)
           (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z2)
           (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M y2 z1 z2 h))))
  (transportb
     (mor_disp ((xx1 ⊗⊗_{ DT} yy1) ⊗⊗_{ DT} zz1)
        (xx2 ⊗⊗_{ DT} (yy2 ⊗⊗_{ DT} zz2)))
     (maponpaths
        (compose
           (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M z1
              (bifunctor_on_objects M x1 y1)
              (bifunctor_on_objects M x2 y1)
              (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M y1 x1 x2
                 f)))
        (cancel_postcomposition
           (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M z1
              (bifunctor_on_objects M x2 y1)
              (bifunctor_on_objects M x2 y2)
              (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M x2 y1 y2
                 g) · α^{ M }_{ x2, y2, z1})
           (α^{ M }_{ x2, y1, z1}
            · leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M x2
                (bifunctor_on_objects M y1 z1)
                (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z1)
                (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M z1 y1
                   y2 g))
           (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M x2
              (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z1)
              (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z2)
              (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M y2 z1 z2
                 h))
           (! associatorlaw_natleftright
                (monoidal_associatorlaw M) x2 y1 y2 z1
                g) @
         ! assoc α^{ M }_{ x2, y1, z1}
             (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M x2
                (bifunctor_on_objects M y1 z1)
                (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z1)
                (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M z1 y1
                   y2 g))
             (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M x2
                (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z1)
                (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z2)
                (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M y2 z1
                   z2 h)) @
         maponpaths (compose α^{ M }_{ x2, y1, z1})
           (! bifunctor_leftcomp M x2
                (bifunctor_on_objects M y1 z1)
                (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z1)
                (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z2)
                (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M z1 y1
                   y2 g)
                (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M y2 z1
                   z2 h))))
     (transportb
        (mor_disp ((xx1 ⊗⊗_{ DT} yy1) ⊗⊗_{ DT} zz1)
           (xx2 ⊗⊗_{ DT} (yy2 ⊗⊗_{ DT} zz2)))
        ((assoc
            (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M z1
               (bifunctor_on_objects M x1 y1)
               (bifunctor_on_objects M x2 y1)
               (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M y1 x1
                  x2 f)) α^{ M }_{ x2, y1, z1}
            (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M x2
               (bifunctor_on_objects M y1 z1)
               (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z2)
               (functoronmorphisms1 M g h)) @
          cancel_postcomposition
            (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M z1
               (bifunctor_on_objects M x1 y1)
               (bifunctor_on_objects M x2 y1)
               (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M y1 x1
                  x2 f) · α^{ M }_{ x2, y1, z1})
            (α^{ M }_{ x1, y1, z1}
             · rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M
                 (bifunctor_on_objects M y1 z1) x1 x2
                 f)
            (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M x2
               (bifunctor_on_objects M y1 z1)
               (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z2)
               (functoronmorphisms1 M g h))
            (! associatorlaw_natright
                 (monoidal_associatorlaw M) x1 x2 y1
                 z1 f) @
          ! assoc α^{ M }_{ x1, y1, z1}
              (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M
                 (bifunctor_on_objects M y1 z1) x1 x2
                 f)
              (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms M x2
                 (bifunctor_on_objects M y1 z1)
                 (bifunctor_on_objects M y2 z2)
                 (functoronmorphisms1 M g h))) @
         associator_nat2 M f g h)
        ((ff ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{r} yy1 ;; xx2 ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{l} gg)
         ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{r} zz1 ;; (xx2 ⊗⊗_{ DT} yy2)
                             ⊗⊗^{ DT}_{l} hh ;; dα x2
                                                 y2 z2
                                                 xx2
                                                 yy2
                                                 zz2)))

M: monoidal C
DT: disp_tensor D M

dtr: disp_associator_nat_rightwhisker dα
dtlr: disp_associator_nat_leftrightwhisker dα

yy2: D y2

zz2: D z2

gg: yy1 -->[ g] yy2
hh: zz1 -->[ h] zz2
transportb
  (mor_disp ((xx1 ⊗⊗_{ DT} yy1) ⊗⊗_{ DT} zz1)
     (xx2 ⊗⊗_{ DT} (yy2 ⊗⊗_{ DT} zz2)))
  (assoc
     (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms M z1
        (bifunctor_on_objects M x1 y1)
